# atl command reference

This file is generated by `scripts/gen-docs.sh` from the clap command tree. Do not edit by hand.

## atl

Unified CLI for Atlassian Confluence and Jira

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl [OPTIONS] <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

**Subcommands**

- `confluence` ‚Äî Confluence operations
- `jira` ‚Äî Jira operations
- `init` ‚Äî Initialize configuration file
- `config` ‚Äî Manage configuration profiles
- `completions` ‚Äî Generate shell completion scripts
- `self` ‚Äî Manage the atl binary itself (check/update)
- `api` ‚Äî Make an authenticated REST request against Confluence or Jira
- `browse` ‚Äî Open a Confluence page or Jira issue in the default browser
- `alias` ‚Äî Manage user-defined command aliases
- `auth` ‚Äî Manage authentication ‚Äî login, logout, status, token

### atl confluence

Confluence operations

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl confluence [OPTIONS] <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

**Subcommands**

- `read` ‚Äî Read a page by ID
- `info` ‚Äî Get page metadata
- `search` ‚Äî Search pages with CQL
- `space` ‚Äî List spaces
- `children` ‚Äî List child pages
- `create` ‚Äî Create a new page
- `update` ‚Äî Update an existing page
- `delete` ‚Äî Delete a page
- `attachment` ‚Äî Attachment operations
- `find` ‚Äî Find pages by title
- `export` ‚Äî Export a page with attachments to a local directory
- `copy-tree` ‚Äî Copy a page tree to another space/parent
- `property` ‚Äî Content property operations
- `label` ‚Äî Label management
- `blog` ‚Äî Blog post management
- `versions` ‚Äî Page version history
- `version-detail` ‚Äî Get a specific page version
- `likes` ‚Äî Page likes
- `operations` ‚Äî Page operations/permissions
- `ancestors` ‚Äî Page ancestors
- `descendants` ‚Äî Page descendants
- `footer-comment` ‚Äî Footer comment management (v2)
- `inline-comment` ‚Äî Inline comment management (v2)
- `whiteboard` ‚Äî Whiteboard management
- `database` ‚Äî Database management
- `folder` ‚Äî Folder management
- `custom-content` ‚Äî Custom content management
- `task` ‚Äî Task management
- `admin-key` ‚Äî Admin key management
- `classification` ‚Äî Content classification management
- `user` ‚Äî Confluence user operations
- `convert-ids` ‚Äî Convert content IDs between formats
- `app-property` ‚Äî App property management
- `page-list` ‚Äî List pages (v2)
- `update-title` ‚Äî Update page title only
- `likes-count` ‚Äî Get like count for a page
- `likes-users` ‚Äî Get users who liked a page
- `page-custom-content` ‚Äî List custom content in a page
- `redact` ‚Äî Redact content from a page

#### atl confluence read

Read a page by ID

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl confluence read [OPTIONS] <PAGE_ID>
```

**Options**

- `<PAGE_ID>` ‚Äî Page ID
- `--body-format` ‚Äî Body format
- `--no-directives` ‚Äî Strip MyST-style directives (`:::info`/`:::warning`/etc.) from markdown output. No effect when `--body-format` is not `markdown`
- `--include-labels` ‚Äî Include labels in the response
- `--include-properties` ‚Äî Include properties in the response
- `--include-operations` ‚Äî Include operations in the response
- `--include-versions` ‚Äî Include version details in the response
- `--include-collaborators` ‚Äî Include collaborators in the response
- `--include-favorited-by` ‚Äî Include favorited-by info in the response
- `--web` ‚Äî Open the page in a browser instead of printing
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

##### atl confluence space create

Create a space

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl confluence space create [OPTIONS] --key <KEY> --name <NAME>
```

**Options**

- `--key, -k` ‚Äî Space key
- `--name, -n` ‚Äî Space name
- `--description, -d` ‚Äî Space description
- `--private` ‚Äî Create as a private (personal) space
- `--alias` ‚Äî Space alias
- `--template-key` ‚Äî Template key to use for the space homepage
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors

##### atl confluence space set-role-assignments

Set space role assignments

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl confluence space set-role-assignments [OPTIONS] --body <BODY> <SPACE_ID>
```

**Options**

- `<SPACE_ID>` ‚Äî Space ID
- `--body, -b` ‚Äî Role assignments (JSON). Use @file to read from file, or - for stdin
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output

###### atl confluence space property list

List properties

**Usage**


#### atl confluence children

List child pages

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl confluence children [OPTIONS] <PAGE_ID>
```

**Options**

- `<PAGE_ID>` ‚Äî Page ID
- `--limit, -l` ‚Äî Max results
- `--depth, -d` ‚Äî Recursion depth (1 = direct children only)
- `--tree` ‚Äî Display as an indented tree
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors

#### atl confluence create

Create a new page

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl confluence create [OPTIONS] --title <TITLE> --body <BODY>
```

**Options**

- `--space, -s` ‚Äî Space key (resolved to ID internally)
- `--space-id` ‚Äî Space ID (numeric, skips key-to-ID lookup)
- `--title, -t` ‚Äî Page title
- `--body, -b` ‚Äî Page body. Use @file to read from file, or - for stdin
- `--parent` ‚Äî Parent page ID
- `--input-format` ‚Äî Input format for the body
- `--private` ‚Äî Create as a private (personal) page
- `--subtype` ‚Äî Page subtype (e.g. "page", "blog")
- `--embedded` ‚Äî Create as embedded content
- `--root-level` ‚Äî Create at root level (no parent)
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

- `--filename` ‚Äî Filter by filename
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors

#### atl confluence export

Export a page with attachments to a local directory

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl confluence export [OPTIONS] <PAGE_ID>
```

**Options**

- `<PAGE_ID>` ‚Äî Page ID
- `--output-dir, -o` ‚Äî Output directory (default: current directory)
- `--body-format` ‚Äî Body format for the page content
- `--no-directives` ‚Äî Strip MyST-style directives (`:::info`/`:::warning`/etc.) from markdown output. No effect when `--body-format` is not `markdown`
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

#### atl confluence copy-tree

Copy a page tree to another space/parent

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl confluence copy-tree [OPTIONS] <SOURCE_PAGE_ID>
```

**Options**

- `<SOURCE_PAGE_ID>` ‚Äî Source page ID (root of the tree to copy)
- `--target-space` ‚Äî Target space key (resolved to ID internally)
- `--target-space-id` ‚Äî Target space ID (numeric, skips key-to-ID lookup)
- `--target-parent` ‚Äî Target parent page ID
- `--depth, -d` ‚Äî Maximum depth to copy (0 = source page only)
- `--dry-run` ‚Äî Show what would be copied without making changes
- `--exclude` ‚Äî Glob pattern to exclude pages by title
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

**Subcommands**

- `list` ‚Äî List blog posts
- `read` ‚Äî Read a blog post
- `create` ‚Äî Create a blog post
- `update` ‚Äî Update a blog post
- `delete` ‚Äî Delete a blog post
- `attachments` ‚Äî List blog post attachments (v2)
- `labels` ‚Äî List blog post labels (v2)
- `footer-comments` ‚Äî List blog post footer comments (v2)
- `inline-comments` ‚Äî List blog post inline comments (v2)
- `versions` ‚Äî List blog post versions (v2)
- `likes` ‚Äî Blog post likes (v2)
- `operations` ‚Äî Blog post operations (v2)
- `version-details` ‚Äî Get specific blog post version details (v2)
- `likes-count` ‚Äî Get like count for a blog post (v2)
- `likes-users` ‚Äî Get users who liked a blog post (v2)
- `custom-content` ‚Äî List custom content in a blog post (v2)
- `redact` ‚Äî Redact content from a blog post (v2)
- `property` ‚Äî Blog post property management (v2)

##### atl confluence blog read

Read a blog post

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl confluence blog read [OPTIONS] <BLOG_ID>
```

**Options**

- `<BLOG_ID>` ‚Äî Blog post ID
- `--body-format` ‚Äî Body format
- `--no-directives` ‚Äî Strip MyST-style directives (`:::info`/`:::warning`/etc.) from markdown output. No effect when `--body-format` is not `markdown`
- `--include-labels` ‚Äî Include labels in the response
- `--include-properties` ‚Äî Include properties in the response
- `--include-operations` ‚Äî Include operations in the response
- `--include-versions` ‚Äî Include version details in the response
- `--include-collaborators` ‚Äî Include collaborators in the response
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager

##### atl confluence blog create

Create a blog post

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl confluence blog create [OPTIONS] --title <TITLE> --body <BODY>
```

**Options**

- `--space, -s` ‚Äî Space key (resolved to ID internally)
- `--space-id` ‚Äî Space ID (numeric, skips key-to-ID lookup)
- `--title, -t` ‚Äî Blog post title
- `--body, -b` ‚Äî Blog post body. Use @file to read from file, or - for stdin
- `--input-format` ‚Äî Input format for the body
- `--private` ‚Äî Create as a private (personal) blog post
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

##### atl confluence footer-comment list

List footer comments for a page

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl confluence footer-comment list [OPTIONS] <PAGE_ID>
```

**Options**

- `<PAGE_ID>` ‚Äî Page ID
- `--limit, -l` ‚Äî Max results
- `--body-format` ‚Äî Body format for the comment body field in the response
- `--no-directives` ‚Äî Strip MyST-style directives (`:::info`/`:::warning`/etc.) from markdown output. No effect when `--body-format` is not `markdown`
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file


- `--limit, -l` ‚Äî Max results
- `--resolution-status` ‚Äî Filter by resolution status (open, resolved, dangling)
- `--body-format` ‚Äî Body format for the comment body field in the response
- `--no-directives` ‚Äî Strip MyST-style directives (`:::info`/`:::warning`/etc.) from markdown output. No effect when `--body-format` is not `markdown`

- `worklog` ‚Äî Worklog management
- `filter` ‚Äî Saved filter management
- `attach` ‚Äî Attach a file to an issue
- `watch` ‚Äî Watch an issue
- `unwatch` ‚Äî Unwatch an issue

- `vote` ‚Äî Vote for an issue
- `unvote` ‚Äî Remove your vote from an issue

- `priority` ‚Äî Priority management

- `automation` ‚Äî Manage Jira Cloud automation rules

#### atl jira search

Search issues with JQL

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl jira search [OPTIONS] [JQL]
```

**Options**

- `<JQL>` ‚Äî JQL query (combined with filter flags via AND)
- `--limit, -l` ‚Äî Max results per page
- `--all` ‚Äî Fetch all results (auto-paginate)
- `--fields, -f` ‚Äî Fields to return (comma-separated)
- `--status` ‚Äî Filter by status name (e.g. "Open", "In Progress")
- `--priority` ‚Äî Filter by priority name
- `--assignee` ‚Äî Filter by assignee (account ID or "currentUser()")
- `--reporter` ‚Äî Filter by reporter
- `--type` ‚Äî Filter by issue type (e.g. Bug, Task, Story)
- `--label` ‚Äî Filter by label
- `--component` ‚Äî Filter by component
- `--resolution` ‚Äî Filter by resolution
- `--created` ‚Äî Filter: created on or after date (YYYY-MM-DD)
- `--created-after` ‚Äî Filter: created after date (YYYY-MM-DD)
- `--updated` ‚Äî Filter: updated on or after date (YYYY-MM-DD)
- `--updated-after` ‚Äî Filter: updated after date (YYYY-MM-DD)
- `--watching` ‚Äî Only issues you are watching
- `--order-by` ‚Äî Order results by field (e.g. "created", "priority")
- `--reverse` ‚Äî Reverse sort order (use with --order-by)
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

#### atl jira view

View an issue

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl jira view [OPTIONS] <KEY>
```

**Options**

- `<KEY>` ‚Äî Issue key (e.g. PROJ-123)
- `--web` ‚Äî Open the issue in a browser instead of printing
- `--body-format` ‚Äî Output format for description and comment bodies
- `--no-directives` ‚Äî Strip MyST-style directives (`:::info`/`:::warning`/etc.) from markdown output. No effect when `--body-format` is not `markdown`
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file

- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

#### atl jira create

Create a new issue

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl jira create [OPTIONS] --project <PROJECT> --issue-type <ISSUE_TYPE> --summary <SUMMARY>
```

**Options**

- `--project` ‚Äî Project key
- `--issue-type, -t` ‚Äî Issue type (e.g. Task, Bug, Story)
- `--summary, -s` ‚Äî Summary
- `--description, -d` ‚Äî Description
- `--assignee` ‚Äî Assignee account ID
- `--priority` ‚Äî Priority name
- `--labels` ‚Äî Labels (comma-separated)
- `--parent` ‚Äî Parent issue key (for subtasks)
- `--fix-version` ‚Äî Fix version(s), comma-separated
- `--component` ‚Äî Component(s), comma-separated
- `--custom` ‚Äî Custom field (repeatable), e.g. --custom customfield_10001=value
- `--input-format` ‚Äî Input format for the body
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

- `--end-date` ‚Äî End date (ISO 8601)

- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

#### atl jira link

Link two issues

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl jira link [OPTIONS] --link-type <LINK_TYPE> <INWARD_KEY> <OUTWARD_KEY>
```

**Options**

- `--link-type, -t` ‚Äî Link type name (e.g. "Blocks", "Duplicates")
- `<INWARD_KEY>` ‚Äî Inward issue key
- `<OUTWARD_KEY>` ‚Äî Outward issue key
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors

- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

#### atl jira field

Field management

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl jira field [OPTIONS] <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

**Subcommands**

- `list` ‚Äî List all fields
- `create` ‚Äî Create a custom field
- `delete` ‚Äî Delete a custom field
- `trash` ‚Äî Move a custom field to trash
- `restore` ‚Äî Restore a custom field from trash
- `context` ‚Äî Manage custom field contexts
- `options` ‚Äî Manage select-list options for a custom field context

- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use

- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

**Subcommands**

- `list` ‚Äî List contexts for the field

- `add-issue-types` ‚Äî Add issue types to a context
- `remove-issue-types` ‚Äî Remove issue types from a context

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl jira field context <FIELD_ID> remove-issue-types [OPTIONS] --issue-type-id <ID> <CONTEXT_ID>
```

**Options**

- `<CONTEXT_ID>` ‚Äî Context ID
- `--issue-type-id` ‚Äî Issue type ID(s) (repeatable, at least one)
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

##### atl jira field options

Manage select-list options for a custom field context

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl jira field options [OPTIONS] <FIELD_ID> <CONTEXT_ID> <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `<FIELD_ID>` ‚Äî Custom field ID (e.g. "customfield_10010")
- `<CONTEXT_ID>` ‚Äî Context ID
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

**Subcommands**

- `list` ‚Äî List options in the context
- `add` ‚Äî Add one or more options
- `update` ‚Äî Update a single option
- `delete` ‚Äî Delete a single option
- `reorder` ‚Äî Reorder options within the context

###### atl jira field options list

**Options**

- `--all` ‚Äî Fetch all results (auto-paginate)
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file

###### atl jira field options reorder

Reorder options within the context

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl jira field options <FIELD_ID> <CONTEXT_ID> reorder [OPTIONS] <--after <ID>|--position <POSITION>> <OPTION_IDS>...
```

**Options**

- `<OPTION_IDS>` ‚Äî Option IDs to move (in the order they should appear)
- `--after` ‚Äî Insert the moved options after this option ID
- `--position` ‚Äî Move the options to a fixed position
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

#### atl jira notify

Send a notification about an issue

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl jira notify [OPTIONS] --subject <SUBJECT> --body <BODY> <KEY>
```

**Options**

- `<KEY>` ‚Äî Issue key (e.g. PROJ-123)
- `--subject, -s` ‚Äî Notification subject
- `--body, -b` ‚Äî Notification body. Use @file to read from file, or - for stdin
- `--to` ‚Äî Recipient account IDs (repeatable)
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager

**Subcommands**

#### atl jira automation

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl jira automation [OPTIONS] <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors

**Subcommands**

- `list` ‚Äî List automation rules
- `get` ‚Äî Get full definition of a rule by UUID

- `update` ‚Äî Update an existing rule with a JSON body
- `enable` ‚Äî Enable a rule
- `disable` ‚Äî Disable a rule
- `delete` ‚Äî Delete a rule (must be disabled first per Atlassian)

- `update` ‚Äî Download and replace the current binary with the latest release

```text
Usage: atl self check [OPTIONS]
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)

#### atl self update

Download and replace the current binary with the latest release

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl self update [OPTIONS]
```

**Options**

- `--to` ‚Äî Install a specific version instead of latest (e.g. 2026.16.2)
- `--allow-downgrade` ‚Äî Permit downgrading when --to points at an older version
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

### atl api

Make an authenticated REST request against Confluence or Jira

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl api [OPTIONS] --service <SERVICE> <ENDPOINT>
```

**Options**

- `<ENDPOINT>` ‚Äî REST endpoint path (e.g. `rest/api/2/myself`). Leading slash optional
- `--service` ‚Äî Which Atlassian product to target
- `--method, -X` ‚Äî HTTP method (default: GET)
- `--header, -H` ‚Äî Custom header in the form `KEY:VALUE`. Repeatable
- `--field, -f` ‚Äî String field in the JSON body, `KEY=VALUE`. `VALUE` may be `@file` to read the contents of a file, or `-` to read stdin. Repeatable. Mutually exclusive with `--input`
- `--raw-field` ‚Äî Raw JSON field in the JSON body, `KEY=VALUE`. `VALUE` is parsed as JSON (e.g. `--raw-field count=42`, `--raw-field tags=[1,2,3]`). Repeatable. Mutually exclusive with `--input`. No short form because `-F` is reserved for `--format`
- `--input` ‚Äî Read the request body verbatim from a file, or `-` for stdin. Mutually exclusive with `--field` / `--raw-field`
- `--query` ‚Äî Query parameter in the form `KEY=VALUE`. Repeatable. No short form because `-q` is reserved for `--quiet`
- `--paginate` ‚Äî Auto-follow pagination until the server reports no more pages
- `--max-pages` ‚Äî Maximum number of pages to fetch when --paginate is set. Defaults to 1000. Use 0 for no limit (not recommended)
- `--preview` ‚Äî Print the constructed request to stderr and exit without sending
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

### atl browse

**Subcommands**

- `list` ‚Äî List all configured aliases
- `delete` ‚Äî Delete an alias

#### atl alias set

Create or update an alias

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl alias set [OPTIONS] <NAME> <EXPANSION>
```

**Options**

- `<NAME>` ‚Äî Alias name (invoked as `atl <name>`)
- `<EXPANSION>` ‚Äî Expansion. Supports shell-style quoting, e.g. `'jira search "project=FOO"'`
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

### atl auth

Manage authentication ‚Äî login, logout, status, token

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl auth [OPTIONS] <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` ‚Äî Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

**Subcommands**

- `login` ‚Äî Log in to Confluence or Jira and store the token in the OS keyring
- `logout` ‚Äî Remove stored credentials for a profile/service
- `status` ‚Äî Show which profiles/services are authenticated
- `token` ‚Äî Print the resolved API token to stdout

#### atl auth login

Log in to Confluence or Jira and store the token in the OS keyring

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl auth login [OPTIONS]
```

**Options**

- `--service` ‚Äî Service to log in to (defaults to both)
- `--profile` ‚Äî Profile name (overrides the global --profile for this login)
- `--domain` ‚Äî Atlassian domain (e.g. acme.atlassian.net). Prompted when omitted
- `--email` ‚Äî Email address for Basic auth. Prompted when omitted and --auth-type=basic
- `--auth-type` ‚Äî Authentication mechanism (basic = email + API token, bearer = PAT)
- `--with-token` ‚Äî Read the token from stdin instead of prompting interactively
- `--skip-verify` ‚Äî Skip the live verification request against the Atlassian API
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

#### atl auth logout

Remove stored credentials for a profile/service

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl auth logout [OPTIONS]
```

**Options**

- `--service` ‚Äî Service to log out of (defaults to both)
- `--profile` ‚Äî Profile name (overrides the global --profile for this logout)
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

#### atl auth status

Show which profiles/services are authenticated

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl auth status [OPTIONS]
```

**Options**

- `--profile` ‚Äî Show status for this profile only (defaults to all)
- `--skip-verify` ‚Äî Skip the live verification request against the Atlassian API
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)

#### atl auth token

Print the resolved API token to stdout

**Usage**

```text
Usage: atl auth token [OPTIONS]
```

**Options**

- `--service` ‚Äî Which service's token to print (required)
- `--profile` ‚Äî Profile name (overrides the global --profile)
- `--force` ‚Äî Print the token even when stdout is a TTY
- `--verbose, -v` ‚Äî Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` ‚Äî Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` ‚Äî Path to configuration file
- `--format, -F` ‚Äî Output format
- `--no-color` ‚Äî Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` ‚Äî Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` ‚Äî Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` ‚Äî Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` ‚Äî Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
- `--retry-all-methods` ‚Äî Retry all HTTP methods, not just GET/HEAD/OPTIONS. May cause duplicate writes on transient failures (a POST that creates a resource may run twice)
